It takes 30 minutes from getting off the bus to the hotel to check in smoothly.
There are really many people in Wuzhen in summer, but the moment you step into the museum, you feel cool and quiet, like two worlds. Our room is on the second floor, and we can see the greenery through the window. It really has the charm of an ancient town. After checking in, taste the hotel's tremella sweet soup and fruits, take a short rest, and visit the Xizha Scenic Area in the twilight. Change the stereotype of scenic area recipes. After dinner, we went to the hotel for a little night tour, took photos of the night view, and returned to the room satisfied.
